(Nasdaq&#58; LUNR, &#8220;Intuitive Machines,&#8221; or the &#8220;Company&#8221;), a leading space exploration, infrastructure, and services company, today announced its financial results for the second quarter ended June&#160;30, 2023.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">Intuitive Machines CEO Steve Altemus said, &#8220;During the second quarter, we were laser-focused on the final assembly process in preparing IM-1 for launch. The Company has secured a launch window from pad 39A, preserving a six-day launch window starting on November 15</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:6.5pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%;position:relative;top:-3.5pt;vertical-align:baseline">th</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">.&#8221; </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">Mr. Altemus continued, &#8220;Progress continues throughout the Company&#59; we&#8217;re building the primary IM-2 structure, integrating payloads and mechanisms to the second lander&#59; while the Company transitions into its new Lunar Production and Operations Center at the Houston Spaceport. The City of Houston and the Houston Airport System helped finance the Company&#8217;s $40 million facility, designed to support NASA&#8217;s $93 billion Artemis program and growing commercial demand for space products and infrastructure, orbital services, lunar access services, and lunar data services.&#8221;</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font This is not a result of the loss of any anticipated material government customer commitments or contract awards.  </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:107%">Mr. Altemus stated, &#8220;While we continue to work toward our milestones, the Company is taking steps to positively mitigate the effects of outside-controlled program delays and higher-priority launch pad congestion while retaining the integrity of our long-term growth plan. Concurrently, we are also pursuing opportunities to diversify the Company&#8217;s revenue streams. We have submitted more than $3 billion in proposals spread across the aerospace and defense sectors, including human spaceflight.&#8221; </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div style="margin-top:8pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:107%">Conference Call Information</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:107%">Intuitive Machines will host a conference call today, August&#160;14, 2023, at 4&#58;30 pm Eastern Time to discuss these results. A webcast replay will be available through the same link on the investors portion of the Intuitive Machines&#8217; website at </font><font style="color:#0000ff;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:107%">https&#58;&#47;&#47;investors.intuitivemachines.com</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:107%">.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div id="if614838e679f46c6a391c96ff9f77d57_10"></div><div style="margin-top:8pt;text-align:justify"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Key Business Metrics and Non-GAAP Financial Measures</font></div><div style="text-align:justify"><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">In addition to the GAAP financial measures set forth in this press release, the Company has included certain financial measures that have not been prepared in accordance with generally accepted accounting principles (&#8220;GAAP&#8221;) and constitute &#8220;non-GAAP financial measures&#8221; as defined by the SEC. This includes adjusted EBITDA (&#8220;Adjusted EBITDA&#8221;).</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div style="text-align:justify"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Adjusted EBITDA is a key performance measure that our management team uses to assess the Company&#8217;s operating performance and is calculated as net income (loss) excluding results from non-operating sources including interest income, interest expense, gain on extinguishing of debt, share based compensation, change in fair value instruments, depreciation, and provision for income taxes. Intuitive Machines has included Adjusted EBITDA because we believe it is helpful in highlighting trends in the Company&#8217;s operating results and because it is frequently used by analysts, investors, and other interested parties to evaluate companies in our industry.</font></div><div style="text-align:justify"><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Adjusted EBITDA has limitations as an analytical measure, and investors should not consider it in isolation or as a substitute for analysis of the Company&#8217;s results as reported under GAAP. Other companies, including companies in Intuitive Machines&#8217; industry, may calculate Adjusted EBITDA differently, which reduces its usefulness as a comparative measure. Because of these limitations, you should consider Adjusted EBITDA alongside other financial performance measures, including various cash flow metrics, net income (loss) and our other GAAP results.  A reconciliation of Adjusted EBITDA to the most directly comparable GAAP financial measure is included below under the heading &#8220;Reconciliation of GAAP to Non-GAAP Financial Measure.&#8221; </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">The Company has also included contracted backlog, which is defined as the total estimate of the revenue the Company expects to realize in the future as a result of performing work on awarded contracts, less the amount of revenue the </font></div><div style="height:40.5pt;position:relative;width:100%"><div style="bottom:0;position:absolute;width:100%"><div><font><br></font></div></div></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"><div style="min-height:40.5pt;width:100%"><div><font><br></font></div></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Company has previously recognized. Intuitive Machines monitors its backlog because we believe it is a forward-looking indicator of potential sales which can be helpful to investors in evaluating the performance of its business and identifying trends over time.  </font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div id="if614838e679f46c6a391c96ff9f77d57_13"></div><div><font style="color:#191818;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:112%">About Intuitive Machines</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#191818;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">Intuitive Machines is a diversified space company focused on space exploration. Intuitive Machines supplies space products and services to support sustained robotic and human exploration to the Moon, Mars, and beyond. Intuitive Machines&#8217; products and services are offered through its four business units&#58; Lunar Access Services, Orbital Services, Lunar Data Services, and Space Products and Infrastructure. For more information, please visit </font><font style="color:#0000ff;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">intuitivemachines.com</font><font style="color:#191818;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">.</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div style="margin-top:8pt"><font style="color:#191818;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:112%">Forward-Looking Statements</font></div><div><font><br></font></div><div><font style="color:#191818;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">This press release includes &#34;forward-looking statements&#34; within the meaning of the Private Securities Litigation Reform Act of 1995, as amended. 0;text-align:right;vertical-align:bottom"></td></tr></table></div><div id="if614838e679f46c6a391c96ff9f77d57_34"></div><div style="margin-top:10pt;text-align:justify"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:700;line-height:120%">Free Cash Flow</font></div><div style="margin-top:8pt;text-align:justify"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">We define free cash flow as net cash (used in) provided by operating activities less purchases of property and equipment. We believe that free cash flow is a meaningful indicator of liquidity that provides information to management and investors about the amount of cash generated from operations that, after purchases of property and equipment, can be used for strategic initiatives, including continuous investment in our business and strengthening our balance sheet.</font></div><div style="margin-top:8pt;text-align:justify"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Free Cash Flow has limitations as a liquidity measure, and you should not consider it in isolation or as a substitute for analysis of our cash flows as reported under GAAP. Some of these limitations are&#58;</font></div><div style="margin-top:8pt;padding-left:45pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-22.5pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:19pt">Free Cash Flow is not a measure calculated in accordance with GAAP and should not be considered in isolation from, or as a substitute for financial information prepared in accordance with GAAP. </font></div><div style="margin-top:8pt;padding-left:45pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-22.5pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:19pt">Free Cash Flow may not be comparable to similarly titled metrics of other companies due to differences among methods of calculation. </font></div><div style="margin-top:8pt;padding-left:45pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:-22.5pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8226;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:19pt">Free Cash Flow may be affected in the near to medium term by the timing of capital investments, fluctuations in our growth and the effect of such fluctuations on working capital and changes in our cash conversion cycle.</font></div><div style="margin-top:8pt;text-align:justify"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">The following table presents a reconciliation of net cash used in operating activities, the most directly comparable financial measure presented in accordance with GAAP, to free cash flow&#58;</font></div><div style="text-align:justify"><table
